[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA one-byte stack buffer overflow was detected in the BER dissector of Wireshark. [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer reports that `dissect_ber_GeneralString` writes past the bounds of[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma stack-allocated buffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`name_string`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in `try_dissect_unknown_ber` within [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`packet-ber.c`. This issue was uncovered by the `handler_ber` fuzz target under [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibFuzzer.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue type: stack-buffer-overflow  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability class: stack-based buffer overflow  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The crash occurs when `dissect_ber_GeneralString` attempts to copy or terminate a[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mGeneralString into a fixed-size stack buffer. AddressSanitizer flags a write of [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbyte beyond the lower bound of the `name_string` array in the caller frame [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`try_dissect_unknown_ber`.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Important observations:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The overflow is triggered in the BER dissector code [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`packet-ber.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m at line [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3194[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The local buffer `name_string` is declared in `try_dissect_unknown_ber` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mline [0m[1;36m814[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and spans bytes [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m160[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m240[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. A write targeting offset [0m[1;36m159[0m[39m silently [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munderflows into the red zone.  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The harness entry point is `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` in `fuzzshark.c`, which [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvokes `epan_dissect_run` and ultimately the BER dissector.  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • No heap allocation is involved; the fault is strictly a stack memory [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorruption.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code areas for holistic investigation:[0m                                            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Locate the vulnerable function in epan/dissectors/packet-ber.c around lines [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3174[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m3194[0m[39m, i.e.:[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;35mdissect_ber_GeneralString[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[39m, char *name_string, unsigned name_len[0m[1;39m)[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Remove the signed int8_t tvb_len and all uses of [0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint8[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Delete the declaration “int8_t tvb_len;”.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Delete the call “tvb_len = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint8[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;” and references to [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtvb_len in the memcpy branch.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Introduce an unsigned length variable [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. “guint32 str_len;” or “size_t [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstr_len;”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and initialize it using the actual payload length provided by out_tvb:[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     str_len = [0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length_remaining[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Clamp str_len to at most name_len – [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m to reserve space for the NUL terminator:[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstr_len >= name_len[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         str_len = name_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Copy exactly str_len bytes from the out_tvb into name_string, then [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNUL-terminate:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint8_t*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mname_string, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, str_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mstr_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Retain the surrounding “if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mname_string[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m … [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39m…[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m'\0'[0m[39m; [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m” structure so that:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If name_string is NULL, no copy is attempted.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If out_tvb is NULL [0m[1;39m([0m[39munexpected[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, name_string becomes an empty string.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Leave all other logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mreturn offset, exception handling, and the [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdissect_ber_restricted_string invocation[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m untouched to preserve existing [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctionality.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJustification:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- By using [0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length_remaining[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m we obtain the true decoded [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstring-payload length, eliminating both the misuse of the first payload byte and [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe signed-[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-bit truncation.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Clamping to name_len – [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m prevents any overflow when writing the trailing [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This change confines itself to the single function, does not alter any external [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAPIs, harness, or utility code, and maintains all original dissector behavior for [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnon-fuzz inputs.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Potential side-effects are minimal: GeneralString fields will now always be [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNUL-terminated correctly and will never overflow the caller’s buffer. Existing [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtests for GeneralString dissector output should continue to pass.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No broader code paths are affected, and this pattern matches similar fixes [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39melsewhere in packet-ber.c where [0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length_remaining[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is used for [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPERmitted string dissectors.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mRelevant context code range:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code_range>epan/dissectors/packet-ber.[0m[1;92mc:3174[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3194[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3190[0m[39m:                [0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint8_t*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mname_string, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, name_len-[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3191[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3192[0m[39m:                [0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint8_t*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mname_string, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, tvb_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3193[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3194[0m[39m:            name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtvb_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3195[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3196[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3197[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3198[0m[39m:    return offset;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3199[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview and Root Cause[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The function `dissect_ber_GeneralString` currently reads a signed byte [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tvb_len` from the TVB, then branches on its value to copy up to `name_len-[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` bytes[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minto the stack buffer `name_string`, before zero-terminating at [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtvb_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`. This logic fails for negative or out-of-bounds values, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcausing underflow or overflow. [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The attempted patch correctly replaces the signed [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-bit length with an [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munsigned [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m-bit remaining-length query, but introduced brace misalignment and left [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe function without a guaranteed `return offset;` on all paths.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Strategy to Safely Clamp and Copy[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Mirror the clamping approach used in the unrestricted [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dissect_ber_GeneralString` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m3089[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m3094[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       ```[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlen >= max_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m len = max_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[39m, str, offset, len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       str[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mlen[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       ```[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In the restricted variant, `name_len` is the buffer size [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m[1;36m80[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. We [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould:[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     a[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Query `str_len = [0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length_remaining[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Clamp `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstr_len > name_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m str_len = name_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Copy exactly `str_len` bytes.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     d[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Zero-terminate at `name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mstr_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Precise Patch Steps[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m At the top of `dissect_ber_GeneralString`, replace the declaration[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        `int8_t tvb_len;`[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      with[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        `guint32 str_len;`[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Replace the entire nested logic from `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mname_string[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m [0m[33m...[0m[39m [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` so that the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction reads:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mname_string[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Get all remaining bytes, clamp to buffer, copy, then [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mzero-terminate *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              str_len = [0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length_remaining[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstr_len > name_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  str_len = name_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint8_t*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mname_string, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, str_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[35m/[0m[39m* No output TVB means no data copied *[0m[35m/[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              str_len = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Always zero-terminate at the clamped length *[0m[35m/[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mstr_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Ensure that after closing the `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mname_string[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` block there is exactly one [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`return offset;` and that braces align:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      return offset;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m No changes are made to harness or test code. The function’s signature, return[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtype, and usage by `try_dissect_unknown_ber` remain unchanged.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By unconditionally clamping using an unsigned length, we eliminate off-by-one [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munderflow/overflow.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Zero-termination at index `str_len` guarantees writes occur within `[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m .. [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mname_len-[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This matches the pattern in the unrestricted version, preserving existing [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior for shorter strings.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Restoring the correct brace levels ensures all control paths end in `return [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffset;`, resolving the compile errors.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No harness, fuzzing logic, or external dependencies are modified, preserving [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtests and fuzz targets.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Side-Effects and Mitigations[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If `name_len` were ever zero, `name_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` underflows. However, callers [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malways pass a positive buffer size [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname_string[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, so this [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprecondition holds.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Should future code allow `name_len == [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m`, an additional guard `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mname_len ==[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return offset;` could be added before copying.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The unrestricted `dissect_ber_GeneralString` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m3089[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m3094[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m uses identical [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclamping logic.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The consistent pattern for other BER string dissectors demonstrates safe [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandling via `tvb_reported_length_remaining`.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWith this patch, compilation errors are resolved, buffer-overflow is prevented, and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe function’s behavior remains semantically consistent.  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
